[10:32:33]

@HentaiBot idk

[10:32:52]
[None] HentaiBot
var Wiki = require("wikijs");
var wiki = new Wiki();

var wikiCallback = function(bot, sender, args)
{
	var input = args.join(" ");

	wiki.search(input).then(function(result)
	{
		var page = result.results[0];

		if(typeof page == 'undefined')
		{
			bot.send("No results found!");
			return;
		}

		wiki.page(page).then(function(page)
		{
			page.summary().then(function(summary)
			{
				if(summary.length > 500)
				{
					summary = summary.substring(0, 500) + "...";
				}
				summary += " - " + page.fullurl;

				bot.send(summary);
			});
		});
	});
};

module.exports = { wiki: wikiCallback };

[17:45:01]
[bw7Gkq] Mr_Zhang
```python
import glob
from imp import reload
from os import remove
from time import sleep
packets=[]
class cmd:
    def __init__(self,name,packet,info):
        self.name = name
        self.packet = packet
        self.info = info
def build_importer(packet_name):
    import_file = open('importer.py','w')
    import_file.write('\
import sys\n\
sys.path.append("./commands")\n\
import {}\n\
def load():\n\
    return {}'.format(packet_name.replace(".py","").replace("commands\\",""),packet_name.replace(".py","").replace("commands\\","")))
    import_file.close()
def loadpackets():
    global packets
    for i in glob.glob('commands/*.py'):
        build_importer(i)
        reload(importer)
        imported_packet = importer.load()
        packet = cmd(imported_packet.info.name,imported_packet,imported_packet.info)
        packets.append(packet)
        remove('importer.py')
        sleep(0.8)
    return packets
build_importer('os')
import importer
```

[20:46:29]
[8mT5YX] MaggieIphone
highly effective way of presenting the student with new information.
Situation teaching: teaching a language by presenting a series of
everyday situations.
In this method, little structural grading is possible. The situation
takes precedence over the structures. The patterns that are included arise
naturally out of the situation itself: they have a thematic significance
rather than a structural one. This system has serious drawbacks.
The dialogues which the student hears are refreshingly natural,
but the teaching of basic patterns inevitably becomes much less
controlled.
Structurally controlled situation teaching: teaching a language by
means of a series of everyday situations, while at the same time grading
the structures which are presented.
This method makes use of all the techniques outlined above: structural
grading, contextualization, and situational teaching. In the early stages
it is possible to use very few patterns indeed. This means that the
"situations'
are often unconvincing and barely possible. Despite this disadvantage, it
would seem to be one of the best methods for learning a language, for it is
possible to exercise linguistic control and yet to present new information
in an interesting way.
